# Improving controls with log data

Here's plots of the [comma-steering-control](https://github.com/commaai/comma-steering-control) dataset and the data I've collected so far from the community.
Community log collection is in a limited state; only cars not in the comma-steering-control dataset will be collected for the time being.
I'll update here periodically so log contributors can see which speeds/angles need to be filled out.

Head to the Comma, Community, or SunnyPilot Discord server #tuning (or tunning-nnff) channels if you want to contribute or learn more!

## Table of Contents
- [1 Community vehicle log counts](#current-counts-of-collected-logs) (83718 total)
- [2 Community lateral data](#2-community-lateral-data) (      66 cars)
- [3a Community lateral torque NNFF fits steer command](#3a-community-lateral-torque-nnff-fits-steer-command) (      82 cars)
- [3b Community lateral torque NNFF fits LKA EPS torque](#3b-community-lateral-torque-nnff-fits-lka-eps-torque) (      68 cars)
- [3c Community lateral torque NNFF fits driver torque](#3c-community-lateral-torque-nnff-fits-driver-torque) (      68 cars)
- [3d Community lateral torque NNFF fits driver EPS combined torque](#3d-community-lateral-torque-nnff-fits-driver-eps-combined-torque) (      62 cars)
- [4 Comma lateral data combined firmware](#4-comma-lateral-data-combined-firmware) (     121 cars)
- [5 Comma lateral data separate firmwares](#5-comma-lateral-data-separate-firmwares) (     526 cars)
